  <script>
    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });
  </script>

    $(function() {

      var pageWidth = $(window).width();

      $('#menuToggle input').click(function() {
       $('#menu').toggle();
       $('html, body').toggleClass('noscroll');
      });

      if(typeof(Modernizr) != "undefined" && Modernizr.input.placeholder){
        $("#body").addClass("has-placeholder");
      }

      // messages
      $("div.error_container").delay(1000).animate({
        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

  <script>
    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });

    $(function() {

      var pageWidth = $(window).width();

      $('#menuToggle input').click(function() {
       $('#menu').toggle();
       $('html, body').toggleClass('noscroll');
      });

      if(typeof(Modernizr) != "undefined" && Modernizr.input.placeholder){
        $("#body").addClass("has-placeholder");
      }

      // messages
      $("div.error_container").delay(1000).animate({
        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

  </script>

               url: 'https://freegeoip.app/json/',
               callback: function(done, response) {
                 // This function must parse the 'response' and return the country code, or fail.
                 // If this function doesn't fail correctly, then the next service will not run.
                 // Therefore, it's generally best to add a try {...} catch () {...} block
                 try {
                   var json = JSON.parse(response);
                   // console.log(json.country_code);

    });

    $("#chapter_id, #section_id").change(function(){
      this.form.submit();
    });
  </script>








  <script>
    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });
  </script>

    <script>
    $(function() {

      var pageWidth = $(window).width();

      $('#menuToggle input').click(function() {
       $('#menu').toggle();
       $('html, body').toggleClass('noscroll');
      });

      if(typeof(Modernizr) != "undefined" && Modernizr.input.placeholder){
        $("#body").addClass("has-placeholder");
      }

      // messages
      $("div.error_container").delay(1000).animate({
        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

  </script>

    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });

        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

  </script>

  <script>
    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });
  </script>

    $(function() {

      var pageWidth = $(window).width();

      $('#menuToggle input').click(function() {
       $('#menu').toggle();
       $('html, body').toggleClass('noscroll');
      });

      if(typeof(Modernizr) != "undefined" && Modernizr.input.placeholder){
        $("#body").addClass("has-placeholder");
      }

      // messages
      $("div.error_container").delay(1000).animate({
        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

  </script>

                 // If this function doesn't fail correctly, then the next service will not run.
                 // Therefore, it's generally best to add a try {...} catch () {...} block

  <script>
    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });
  </script>

    $(function() {

      var pageWidth = $(window).width();

      $('#menuToggle input').click(function() {
       $('#menu').toggle();
       $('html, body').toggleClass('noscroll');
      });

      if(typeof(Modernizr) != "undefined" && Modernizr.input.placeholder){
        $("#body").addClass("has-placeholder");
      }

      // messages
      $("div.error_container").delay(1000).animate({
        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

  </script>

  <script>
    $(".inquiry_btn").click(function(){
      var scid = $(this).data("scid");
        if ($("body").hasClass("gcu")) {
          var url = "/reg/signup?iama=S%3A9&require=1";
          var decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(url);
          window.location.href = decodeUrl
        } else {
          var url = "/reg/signup?campaign=schoolconnect&scid=-1".replace("-1", scid);
          window.location.href = url;
        }
      return false;
    });
  </script>

    $(function() {

      var pageWidth = $(window).width();

      $('#menuToggle input').click(function() {
       $('#menu').toggle();
       $('html, body').toggleClass('noscroll');
      });

      if(typeof(Modernizr) != "undefined" && Modernizr.input.placeholder){
        $("#body").addClass("has-placeholder");
      }

      // messages
      $("div.error_container").delay(1000).animate({
        left: '+=380'
      }).delay(7000).animate({
        left: '-=380'
      });

      // slide up message
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-out') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up").slideUp(500);
              var date = new Date();
              var minutes = 120;
              date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
              $.cookie('fb-out', 'true', { expires: date, path: '/' });
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // slide up message logged in
      $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() > 200) {
          if ($.cookie('fb-in') != 'true' ) {
            $(".slide_up_in").slideDown(800);
            $(".close_banner").click(function() {
              $(".slide_up_in").slideUp(500);
              $.cookie('fb-in', 'true', { expires: 7, path: '/'});
              return false;
            });
          }
        }
      });

      // dropdown menus
      var megaConfig = {
             interval: 100,
             sensitivity: 7,
             over: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").show();
          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,
             out: function(){
          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      if ($(window).width() >= 1259) {
        $(".content_category").hoverIntent(megaConfig);
      }

      $("a.tracked, button.tracked").click(function(){
        $(this).removeClass("tracked");
        try{


        }
        catch(e){}
        return true;
      });

      //accordion for footer links
      $('.accordion').click(function() {
        $(this).next('ul').slideToggle();
        $(this).children('.toggle').toggleClass('rotate');
        return false;
      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {
        $('input, select').each(function(){
          if($(this).val()) {
            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }
      });

    });

        } else {

          $(this).addClass('link-category');
         },
             timeout: 300,

          $(this).find("ul").hide();
          $(this).removeClass('link-category');
         }
        };

      }

        catch(e){}

      });

      //offsets for inline anchors
      $('a[href*="#"]:not([href="#"])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//,'') && location.hostname == this.hostname) {
          var target = $(this.hash);
          target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) +']');
          if (target.length) {
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 150
            }, 1000);
            return false;
          }
        }
      });

      //Handle input and selects being style proper evin if autofilled
      setTimeout(function () {

            $(this).addClass('active');
          }
          else if($(this).val() == 188){
            $(this).removeClass('active');
          }
        });
        $('#id_country_id').removeClass('active');
      }, 500);

      $('input, select').change(function() {
        if($(this).val()){
          $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        else{
          $(this).removeClass('active');
        }

                   // console.log(json.country_code);
                   if (json.country_code) {
                     return {code: json.country_code}
                   }
                   throw 'Could not find a country code in the response';
                 } catch (err) {
                   return new Error('Invalid response (' + err + ')');
                 }
               },
             };
           },
         },
         services: ["geolocation"]
      }
    })
  });
</script>


 </body>
</html>
